<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos was a cause of those who came into     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being and he continued all the more to be at a   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>loss and he was astonished.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Instead of perfection, he saw a defect;          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>instead of unification, he saw division;         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>instead of stability, he saw disturbances;       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>instead of rests, tumults.                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Neither was it possible for him to make them     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>cease from loving disturbance, nor was it        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>possible for him to destroy it.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He was completely powerless, once his totality   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and his exaltation abandoned him.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those who had come into being not knowing        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>themselves both did not know the Pleromas from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which they came forth and did not know the one   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who was the cause of their existence.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos, being in such unstable conditions,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>did not continue to bring forth anything like    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>emanations, the things which are in the          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Pleroma, the glories which exist for the honor   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the Father.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Rather, he brought forth little weaklings,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hindered) by the illnesses by which he too was   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hindered.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It was the likeness of the disposition which     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was a unity, that which was the cause of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which do not themselves exist from the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Until the one who brought forth into the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>defect these things which were thus in need,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>until he judged those who came into being        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>because of him contrary to reason - which is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the judgment which became a condemnation - he    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>struggled against them unto destruction, that    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is, the ones who struggled against the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>condemnation and whom the wrath pursues, while   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it (the wrath) accepts and redeems (them) from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their (false) opinion and apostasy, since from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it is the conversion which is also called        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;metanoia.&#34; The Logos turned to another          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>opinion and another thought.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Having turned away from evil, he turned toward   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the good things.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Following the conversion came the thought of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the things which exist and the prayer for the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who converted himself to the good.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The one who is in the Pleroma was what he        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first prayed to and remembered; then (he         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>remembered) his brothers individually and        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(yet) always with one another; then all of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them together; but before all of them, the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The prayer of the agreement was a help for him   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in his own return and (in that of) the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totality, for a cause of his remembering those   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who have existed from the first was his being    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>remembered.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is the thought which calls out from afar,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>bringing him back.                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>All his prayer and remembering were numerous     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>powers according to that limit.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For there is nothing barren in his thought.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The powers were good and were greater than       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the likeness.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For those belonging to the likeness also         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>belong to a nature of falsehood.                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>From an illusion of similarity and a thought     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of arrogance has come about that which they      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>became.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And they originate from the thought which        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first knew them.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>To what do the former beings pertain?            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They are like forgetfulness and heavy sleep;     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being like those who dream troubled dreams, to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom sleep comes while they - those who dream    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>- are oppressed.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The others are like some creatures of light      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for him, looking for the rising of the sun,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since it happened that they saw in him dreams    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which are truly sweet.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It immediately put a stop to the emanations of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the thought.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They did not any longer have their substance     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and also they did not have honor any longer.     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Though he is not equal to those who pre-         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>existed, if they were superior to the            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>likenesses, it was he alone through whom they    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>were more exalted than those, for they are not   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from a good intent.                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It was not from the sickness which came into     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being that they were produced, from which is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the good intent, but (from) the one who sought   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>after the pre-existent.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Once he had prayed, he both raised himself to    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the good and sowed in them a pre-disposition     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to seek and pray to the glorious pre-existent    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one, and he sowed in them a thought about him    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and an idea, so that they should think that      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>something greater than themselves exists prior   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to them, although they did not understand what   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it was.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Begetting harmony and mutual love through that   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought, they acted in unity and unanimity,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since from unity and from unanimity they have    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received their very being.                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They were stronger than them in the lust for     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power, for they were more honored than the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first ones, who had been raised above them.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those had not humbled themselves.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They thought about themselves that they were     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>beings originating from themselves alone and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>were without a source.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As they brought forth at first according to      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their own birth, the two orders assaulted one    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>another, fighting for command because of their   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>manner of being.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As a result, they were submerged in forces and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>natures in accord with the condition of mutual   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>assault, having lust for power and all other     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things of this sort.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is from these that the vain love of glory     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>draws all of them to the desire of the lust      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for power, while none of them has the exalted    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought nor acknowledges it.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The powers of this thought are prepared in the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>works of the pre-existent &lt;ones&gt;, those of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which they are the representations.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For the order of those of this sort had mutual   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>harmony, but it fought against the order of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the likeness, while the order of        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the likeness wages war against the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>representations and acts against it alone,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>because of its wrath.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>From this it [...] them [...] one another,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>many [...] necessity appointed them [...] and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might prevail [...] was not a multitude, [...]   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and their envy and their [...] and their wrath   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and violence and desire and prevailing           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ignorance produce empty matters and powers of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>various sorts, mixed in great number with one    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>another; while the mind of the Logos, who was    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a cause of their begetting, was open to a        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation of the hope which would come to him   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from above.                                      |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos which moved had the hope and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>expectation of him who is exalted.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As for those of the shadow, he separated         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself from them in every way, since they       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fight against him and are not at all humble      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>before him.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He was content with the beings of the thought.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And as for the one who is set up in this way     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and who is within the exalted boundary,          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>remembering the one who is defective, the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Logos brought him forth in an invisible way,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>among those who came into being according to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the thought, according to the one who was with   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them, until the light shone upon him from        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>above as a lifegiver, the one who was begotten   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>by the thought of brotherly love of the pre-     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>existent Pleromas.                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The stumbling, which happened to the aeons of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Father of the Totalities who did not         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>suffer, was brought to them, as if it were       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their own, in a careful and non-malicious and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>immensely sweet way.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It was brought to the Totalities so that they    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might be instructed about the defect by the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>single one, from whom alone they all received    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>strength to eliminate the defects.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The order which was his came into being from     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him who ran on high and that which brought       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>itself forth from him and from the entire        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perfection.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The one who ran on high became for the one who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was defective an intercessor with the            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>emanation of the aeons which had come into       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being in accord with the things which exist.     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>When he prayed to them, they consented           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>joyously and willingly, since they were in       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>agreement, and with harmonious consent, to aid   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the defective one.                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They gathered together, asking the Father with   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>beneficent intent that there be aid from         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>above, from the Father, for his glory, since     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the defective one could not become perfect in    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>any other way, unless it was the will of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Pleroma of the Father, which he had drawn to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself, revealed, and given to the defective    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one.                                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Then from the harmony, in a joyous willingness   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which had come into being, they brought forth    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the fruit, which was a begetting from the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>harmony, a unity, a possession of the            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totalities, revealing the countenance of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father, of whom the aeons thought as they gave   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glory and prayed for help for their brother      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with a wish in which the Father counted          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself with them.                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Thus, it was willingly and gladly that they      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>bring forth the fruit.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And he made manifest the agreement of the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation of his union with them, which is      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>his beloved Son.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But the Son in whom the Totalities are pleased   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>put himself on them as a garment, through        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which he gave perfection to the defective one,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and gave confirmation to those who are           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perfect, the one who is properly called          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;Savior&#34; and &#34;the Redeemer&#34; and &#34;the Well-       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Pleasing one&#34; and &#34;the Beloved,&#34; &#34;the one to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom prayers have been offered&#34; and &#34;the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Christ&#34; and &#34;the Light of those appointed,&#34; in   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>accordance with the ones from whom he was        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth, since he has become the names     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the positions which were given to him.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Yet, what other name may be applied to him       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>except &#34;the Son,&#34; as we previously said, since   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he is the knowledge of the Father, whom he       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>wanted them to know?                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Not only did the aeons generate the              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>countenance of the Father to whom they gave      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>praise, which was written previously, but also   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they generated their own; for the aeons who      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>give glory generated their countenance and       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their face.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They were produced as an army for him, as for    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a king, since the beings of the thought have a   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>powerful fellowship and an intermingled          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>harmony.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They came forth in a multifaceted form, in       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>order that the one to whom help was to be        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>given might see those to whom he had prayed      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for help.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He also sees the one who gave it to him.         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The fruit of the agreement with him, of which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>we previously spoke, is subject to the power     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the Totalities.                               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For the Father has set the Totalities within     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him, both the ones which pre-exist and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ones which are, and the ones which will be.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He was capable (of doing it).                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He revealed those which he had placed within     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him.                                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He did not give them, when he entrusted them     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to him.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He directed the organization of the universe     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>according to the authority which was given him   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from the first and (according to) the power of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the task.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Thus, he began and effected his revelation.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The one in whom the Father is and the one in     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom the Totalities are &lt;was&gt; created before     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the one who lacked sight.                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He instructed him about those who searched for   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their sight, by means of the shining of that     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perfect light.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He first perfected him in ineffable joy.         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He perfected him for himself as a perfect one    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and he also gave him what is appropriate to      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>each individual.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For this is the determination of the first       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>joy.                                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And &lt;he&gt; sowed in him in an invisible way a      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>word which is destined to be knowledge.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And he gave him power to separate and cast out   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from himself those who are disobedient to him.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Thus, he made himself manifest to him.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But to those who came into being because of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him he revealed a form surpassing them.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They acted in a hostile way toward one           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>another.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Suddenly he revealed himself to them,            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>approaching them in the form of lightning.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And in putting an end to the entanglement        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which they have with one another he stopped it   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>by the sudden revelation, which they were not    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>informed about, did not expect, and did not      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>know of.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Because of this, they were afraid and fell       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>down, since they were not able to bear the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>appearance of the light which struck them.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The one who appeared was an assault for the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>two orders.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Just as the beings of thought had been given     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the name &#34;little one,&#34; so they have a faint      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>notion that they have the exalted one, he        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>exists before them, and they have sown within    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them an attitude of amazement at the exalted     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who will become manifest.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, they welcomed his revelation and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they worshipped him.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They became convinced witnesses to &lt;him&gt;.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They acknowledged the light which had come       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>into being as one stronger than those who        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fought against them.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The beings of the likeness, however, were        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>exceedingly afraid, since they were not able     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to hear about him in the beginning, that there   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is a vision of this sort.                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore they fell down to the pit of           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ignorance which is called &#34;the Outer             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Darkness,&#34; and &#34;Chaos&#34; and &#34;Hades&#34; and &#34;the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Abyss.&#34; He set up what was beneath the order     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the beings of thought, as it was stronger     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>than they.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They were worthy of ruling over the              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>unspeakable darkness, since it is theirs and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is the lot which was assigned to them.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He granted them that they, too, should be of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>use for the organization which was to come, to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which he had assigned them.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>There is a great difference between the          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation of the one who came into being to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the one who was defective and to those things    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which are to come into being because of him.     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For he revealed himself to him within him,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since he is with him, is a fellow sufferer       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with him, gives him rest little by little,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>makes him grow, lifts him up, gives himself to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him completely for enjoyment from a vision.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But to those who fall outside, he revealed       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself quickly and in a striking way and he     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>withdrew to himself suddenly without having      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>let them see him.                                |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>When the Logos which was defective was           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>illumined, his Pleroma began.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He escaped those who had disturbed him at        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He became unmixed with them.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He stripped off that arrogant thought.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He received mingling with the Rest, when those   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who had been disobedient to him at first bent    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>down and humbled themselves before him.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And he rejoiced over the visitation of his       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brothers who had visited him.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He gave glory and praise to those who had        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>become manifest as a help to him, while he       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>gave thanks, because he had escaped those who    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revolted against him, and admired and honored    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the greatness and those who had appeared to      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him in a determined way.                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He generated manifest images of the living       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>visages, pleasing among things which are good,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>existing among the things which exist,           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>resembling them in beauty, but unequal to them   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in truth, since they are not from an agreement   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with him, between the one who brought them       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forth and the one who revealed himself to him.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But in wisdom and knowledge he acts, mingling    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Logos with him(self) entirely.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, those which came forth from him are   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>great, just as that which is truly great.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>After he was amazed at the beauty of the ones    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who had appeared to him, he professed            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>gratitude for this visitation.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos performed this activity, through       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those from whom he had received aid, for the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>stability of those who had come into being       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>because of him and so that they might receive    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>something good, since he thought to pray for     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the organization of all those who came forth     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from him, which is stabilized, so that it        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might make them established.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, those whom he intentionally           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>produced are in chariots, just as those who      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>came into being, those who have appeared, so     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that they might pass through every place of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which are below, so that each one might   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>be given the place which is constituted as he    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is.                                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is destruction for the beings of the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>likeness, yet is an act of beneficence for the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>beings of the thought, a revelation              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Dittography of those who are from the            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ordinance, which was a unity while suffering,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>while they are seeds, which have not come to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>be by themselves.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The one who appeared was a countenance of the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father and of the harmony.                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He was a garment (composed) of every grace,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and food which is for those whom the Logos       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth while praying and giving glory     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and honor.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is the one whom he glorified and honored    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>while looking to those to whom he prayed, so     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that he might perfect them through the images    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which he had brought forth.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos added even more to their mutual        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since they have joy and abundant rest and        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>undefiled pleasures.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He generated those whom he remembered at         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>first, when they were not with him, (he          |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Dittography Now, while he who belongs to the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>vision is with him, he exists in hope and        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>faith in the perfect Father, as much as the      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>light, for they cannot accept the great,         |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The thought of the Logos, who had returned to    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Similarly, it is called &#34;Storehouse,&#34; because    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And it is also called &#34;Bride,&#34; because of the    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is also called &#34;Kingdom,&#34; because of the      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mentioned, but in power they are not equal,      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>In this mingling with one another they have      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>equality, but each one has not cast off what     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, they are passions, for passion is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sickness, since they are productions not of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the agreement of the Pleroma, but of this one,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>prematurely, before he received the Father.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Hence, the agreement with his Totality and       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to accommodate their sudden, hasty coming,       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is fitting, from the prayer which he made     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the conversion which occurred because of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it, that some should perish, while others        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>benefit, and still others be set apart.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He first prepared the punishment of those who    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>are disobedient, making use of a power of the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who appeared, the one from whom he           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received authority over all things, so as to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>be separate from him.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He is the one who is below, and he also keeps    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself apart from that which is exalted,        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>until he prepares the organization of all        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those things which are external, and gives to    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>each the place which is assigned to it.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos established him(self) at first, when   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he beautified the Totalities, as a basic         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>principle and cause and ruler of the things      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which came to be, like the Father, the one who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was the cause of the establishment, which was    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the first to exist after him.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He created the pre-existent images, which he     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth in thanks and glorification.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Then he beautified the place of those whom he    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>had brought forth in glory, which is called      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;Paradise&#34; and &#34;the Enjoyment&#34; and &#34;the Joy      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>full of sustenance&#34; and &#34;the Joy,&#34; which pre-    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>exist.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And of every goodness which exists in the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Pleroma, it preserves the image.                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Then he beautified the kingdom, like a city      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>filled with everything pleasing, which is        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brotherly love and the great generosity, which   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is filled with the holy spirits and the mighty   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>powers which govern them, which the Logos        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>produced and established in power.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Then (he beautified) the place of the Church     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which assembles in this place, having the form   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the Church which exists in the aeons, which   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glorifies the Father.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>After these (he beautified) the place of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>faith and obedience (which arises) from hope,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which things the Logos received when the light   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>appeared; then (he beautified the place of)      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the disposition, which is prayer and             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>supplication, which were followed by             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forgiveness and the word concerning the one      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who would appear.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>All the spiritual places are in spiritual        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They are separate from the beings of the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought, since the power is established in an    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>image, which is that which separates the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Pleroma from the Logos, while the power which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is active in prophesying about the things        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which will be, directs the beings of the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought which have come into being toward that   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is pre-existent, and it does not permit    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them to mix with the things which have come      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>into being through a vision of the things        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which are with him.                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The beings of the thought which is outside are   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>humble; they preserve the representation of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the pleromatic, especially because of the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sharing in the names by which they are           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>beautiful.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The conversion is humble toward the beings of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the thought, and the law, too, is humble         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>toward them, (the law) of the judgment, which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is the condemnation and the wrath.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also humble toward them is the power which       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>separates those who fall below them, sends       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them far off and does not allow them to spread   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>out over the beings of the thought and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>conversion, which (power) consists in fear and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perplexity and forgetfulness and astonishment    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and ignorance and the things which have come     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>into being in the manner of a likeness,          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through fantasy.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And these things, too, which were in fact        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>lowly, are given the exalted names.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>There is no knowledge for those who have come    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forth from them with arrogance and lust for      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power and disobedience and falsehood.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>To each one he gave a name, since the two        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>orders are in a name.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those belonging to the thought and those of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the representation are called &#34;the Right Ones&#34;   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and &#34;Psychic&#34; and &#34;the Fiery Ones&#34; and &#34;the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Middle Ones.&#34; Those who belong to the arrogant   |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the aeon of the images pure from all those who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fight against it, since it is a place of joy.    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>However, to those of the thought he revealed     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the thought which he had stripped from           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>himself, desiring to draw them into a material   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>union, for the sake of their system and          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>dwelling place, and in order that they might     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>also bring forth an impulse for diminution       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from their attraction to evil, so that they      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might not any more rejoice in the glory of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their environment and be dissolved, but might    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>rather see their sickness in which they          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>suffer, so that they might beget love and        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>continuous searching after the one who is able   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to heal them of the inferiority.                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also over those who belong to the likeness, he   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>set the word of beauty, so that he might bring   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them into a form.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He also set over them the law of judgment.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Again, he set over them the powers which the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>roots had produced in their lust for power.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He appointed them as rulers over them, so        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that, either by the support of the word which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is beautiful, or by the threat of the law, or    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>by the power of lust for power, the order        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might be preserved from those who have reduced   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it to evil, while the Logos is pleased with      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them, since they are useful for the              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>organization.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Logos knows the agreement in the lust for    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power of the two orders.                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>To these and to all the others, he graciously    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>granted their desire.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He gave to each one the appropriate rank, and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it was ordered that each one be a ruler over a   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>place and an activity.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He yields to the place of the one more exalted   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>than himself, in order to command the other      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>places in an activity which is in the allotted   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>activity which falls to him to have control      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>over because of his mode of being.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As a result, there are commanders and            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>subordinates in positions of domination and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>subjection among the angels and archangels,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>while the activities are of various types and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>are different.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Each one of the archons with his race and his    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perquisites to which his lot has claim, just     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>as they appeared, each was on guard, since       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they have been entrusted with the organization   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and none lacks a command and none is without     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>kingship from the end of the heavens to the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>end of the earth, even to the foundations of     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>There are kings, there are lords and those who   |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>still others for giving rest and healing,        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is characterized by every property and           |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>below, and he uses him as a mouth, to say the    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The things which he has spoken he does.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>When he saw that they were great and good and    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he himself in his own thought had been the one   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to say them and do them, not knowing that the    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>moves him in a determined way toward those       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which he wants.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>places which we mentioned previously in the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>discussion about the images.                     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Not only &lt;did&gt; he work, but also, as the one     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things greater than his own essence.             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Since in his essence he is a &#34;god&#34; and           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;father&#34; and all the rest of the honorific       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>titles, he was thinking that they were           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>elements of his own essence.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He established a rest for those who obey him,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>but for those who disobey him, he also           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>established punishments.                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>With him, too, there is a paradise and a         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>kingdom and everything else which exists in      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the aeon which exists before him.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They are more valuable than the imprints,        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to speak, because he does not see in what way    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>about.                                           |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>are spiritual, though they were of his own       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>essence.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For, thus they were honored in every place by    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him, being pure, from the countenance of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who appointed them, and they were            |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who appointed them.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>After he listened to him in this way,            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>properly, about the lights, which are the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>source and the system, he set them over the      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The invisible spirit moved him in this way, so   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that he would wish to administer through his     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>own servant, whom he too used, as a hand and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>as a mouth and as if he were his face, (and      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with whom he has done what is ignorant might     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The strong powers which the spiritual Logos      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth from fantasy and arrogance, he     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>established in the first spiritual rank.         |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>commands with compulsion and force to the        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>jealousy, and all the other offspring from       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>dispositions of this sort, he set in a servile   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>order controlling the extremities, commanding    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>all those which exist and all (the realm of)     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>generation, from whom come rapidly destroying    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>illnesses, who eagerly desire begetting, who     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>are something in the place where they are from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and to which they will return.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And therefore, he appointed over them            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>authoritative powers, acting continuously on     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>matter, in order that the offspring of those     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which exist might also exist continuously.       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For this is their glory.                         |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>

<h2 id="part-ii">Part II</h2>
<h3 id="11-dot-the-creation-of-material-humanity">11. The Creation of Material Humanity</h3>
<div class="highlight"><div style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;">
<table style="border-spacing:0;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;"><tr><td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">  1
</span><span style="white-space:pre;user-select:none;margin-right:0.4em;padding:0 0.4em 0 0.4em;color:#7f7f7f">  2
