<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The matter which flows through its form (is) a   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>cause by which the invisibility which exists     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through the powers [...] for them all, for       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>[...], as they beget before them and destroy.    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The thought which is set between those of the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>right and those of the left is a power of        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>begetting.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>All those which the first ones will wish to      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>make, so to speak, a projection of theirs,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>like a shadow cast from and following a body,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those things which are the roots of the          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>visible creations, namely, the entire            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>preparation of the adornment of the images and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>representations and likenesses, have come into   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being because of those who need education and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>teaching and formation, so that the smallness    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>might grow, little by little, as through a       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mirror image.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For it was for this reason that he created       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mankind at the end, having first prepared and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>provided for him the things which he had         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>created for his sake.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Like that of all else is the creation of         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mankind as well.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The spiritual Logos moved him invisibly, as he   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perfected him through the Demiurge and his       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>angelic servants, who shared in the act of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fashioning in multitudes, when he took counsel   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with his archons.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Like a shadow is earthly man, so that he might   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>be like those who are cut off from the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totalities.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also he is something prepared by all of them,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the right and those of the left,        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since each one in the orders gives a form to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the [...] in which it exists.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The [...] which the Logos who was defective      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth, who was in the sickness, did      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>not resemble him, because he brought it forth    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forgetfully, ignorantly, and defectively, and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in all the other weak ways, although the Logos   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>gave the first form through the Demiurge out     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of ignorance, so that he would learn that the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>exalted one exists, and would know that he       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is what the prophet called &#34;Living          |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is fitting that we explain about the soul     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it is his, since it is from him, as from a       |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also those of the left brought forth, as it      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>were, men of their own, since they have the      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The spiritual substance is a single thing and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a single representation, and its weakness is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the determination in many forms.                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As for the substance of the psychics, its        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>determination is double, since it has the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>knowledge and the confession of the exalted      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one, and it is not inclined to evil, because     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the inclination of the thought.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As for the material substance, its way is        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>different and in many forms, and it was a        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>weakness which existed in many types of          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>inclination.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The first human being is a mixed formation,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and a mixed creation, and a deposit of those     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the left and those of the right, and a        |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The noble elect substance which is in him was    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>more exalted.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It created and it did not wound them.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore they issued a command, making a        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>threat and bringing upon him a great danger,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is death.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>evil did he allow him to taste, and from the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>other tree with the double (fruit) he did not    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>allow him to eat, much less from the tree of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>life, so that they would not acquire honor       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>[...] them, and so that they would not be        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>[...] by the evil power which is called &#34;the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>serpent.&#34; And he is more cunning than all the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>evil powers.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He led man astray through the determination of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those things which belong to the thought and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the desires.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&lt;He&gt; made him transgress the command, so that    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he would die.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And he was expelled from every enjoyment of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that place.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is the expulsion which was made for him,    |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the things which belong to the likeness and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the representation.                     |

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>If both the orders, those on the right and       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those on the left, are brought together with     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one another by the thought which is set          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>between them, which gives them their             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>organization with each other, it happens that    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they both act with the same emulation of their   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>deeds, with those of the right resembling        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the left, and those of the left         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>resembling those of the right.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And if at times the evil order begins to do      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>evil in a foolish way, the &lt;wise&gt; order          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>emulates, in the form of a man of violence,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>also doing what is evil, as if it were a power   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of a man of violence.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>At other times the foolish order attempts to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>do good, making itself like it, since the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hidden order, too, is zealous to do it.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Just as it is in the things which are            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>established, so (it is) in the things which      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>have come to be.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Since they bring things unlike one another,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those who were not instructed were unable to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>know the cause of the things which exist.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, they have introduced other types      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(of explanation), some saying that it is         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>according to providence that the things which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>exist have their being.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>These are the people who observe the stability   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the conformity of the movement of            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>creation.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that it is something alien.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>These are people who observe the diversity and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the lawlessness and the evil of the powers.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that the things which exist are       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>what is destined to happen.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>These are the people who were occupied with      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>this matter.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that it is something in accordance    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with nature.                                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that it is a self-existent.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The majority, however, all who have reached as   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>far as the visible elements, do not know         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>anything more than them.                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those who were wise among the Greeks and the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>barbarians have advanced to the powers which     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>have come into being by way of imagination and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>vain thought.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those who have come from these, in accord with   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the mutual conflict and rebellious manner        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>active in them, also spoke in a likely,          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>arrogant and imaginary way concerning the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which they thought of as wisdom,          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>although the likeness deceived them, since       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they thought that they had attained the truth,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>when they had (only) attained error.             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(They did so) not simply in minor                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>appellations, but the powers themselves seem     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to hinder them, as if they were the Totality.    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, the order was caught up in fighting   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>itself alone, because of the arrogant            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>hostility of one of the offspring of the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>archon who is superior, who exists before him.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, nothing was in agreement with its     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fellows, nothing, neither philosophy nor types   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of medicine nor types of rhetoric nor types of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>music nor types of logic, but they are           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>opinions and theories.                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Ineffability held sway in confusion, because     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the indescribable quality of those who hold   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sway, who give them thoughts.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Now, as for the things which came forth from     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the &lt;race&gt; of the Hebrews, things which are      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>written by the hylics who speak in the fashion   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the Greeks, the powers of those who think     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>about all of them, so to speak, the &#34;right       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ones,&#34; the powers which move them all to think   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of words and a representation, they &lt;brought&gt;    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them, and they grasped so as to attain the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>truth and used the confused powers which act     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in them.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Afterwards they attained to the order of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>unmixed ones, the one which is established,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the unity which exists as a representation of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the representation of the Father.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is not invisible in its nature, but a         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>wisdom envelops it, so that it might preserve    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the form of the truly invisible one.             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, many angels have not been able to     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>see it.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also, other men of the Hebrew race, of whom we   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>already spoke, namely the righteous ones and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the prophets, did not think of anything and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>did not say anything from imagination or         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through a likeness or from esoteric thinking,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>but each one by the power which was at work in   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him, and while listening to the things which     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he saw and heard, spoke of them in [...].        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They have a unified harmony with one another     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>after the manner of those who worked in them,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since they preserve the connection and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mutual harmony primarily by the confession of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the one more exalted than they.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And there is one who is greater than they, who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was appointed since they have need of him, and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom the spiritual Logos begot along with them   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>as one who needs the exalted one, in hope and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>expectation in accord with the thought which     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is the seed of salvation.                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And he is an illuminating word, which consists   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the thought and his offspring and his         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>emanations.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Since the righteous ones and the prophets,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom we have previously mentioned, preserve      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the confession and the testimony concerning      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the one who is great, made by their fathers      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who were looking for the hope and the hearing,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in them is sown the seed of prayer and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>searching, which is sown in many who have        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>searched for strengthening.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It appears and draws them to love the exalted    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one, to proclaim these things as pertaining to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a unity.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And it was a unity which worked in them when     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they spoke.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Their vision and their words do not differ       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>because of the multitude of those who have       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>given them the vision and the word.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, those who have listened to what       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they have said concerning this do not reject     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>any of it, but have accepted the scriptures in   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>an altered way.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>By interpreting them, they established many      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>heresies which exist to the present among the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Jews.                                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Some say that God is one, who made a             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>proclamation in the ancient scriptures.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that he is many.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Some say that God is simple and was a single     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>mind in nature.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Others say that his activity is linked with      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the establishment of good and evil.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Still others say that he is the creator of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that which has come into being.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Still others say that it was by the angels       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that he created.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The multitude of ideas of this sort is the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>multitude of forms and the abundance of types    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of scripture, that which produced their          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>teachers of the Law.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The prophets, however, did not say anything of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their own accord, but each one of them (spoke)   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of the things which he had seen and heard        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through the proclamation of the Savior.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is what he proclaimed, with the main        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>subject of their proclamation being that which   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>each said concerning the coming of the Savior,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is this coming.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Sometimes the prophets speak about it as if it   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>will be.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Sometimes (it is) as if the Savior speaks from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their mouths, saying that the Savior will come   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and show favor to those who have not known       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him.                                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They have not all joined with one another in     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>confessing anything, but each one, on the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>basis of the thing from which he received        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power to speak about him, and on the basis of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the place which he saw, thinks that it is from   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it that he will be begotten, and that he will    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>come from that place.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Not one of them knew whence he would come nor    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>by whom he would be begotten, but he alone is    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the one of whom it is worthy to speak, the one   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who will be begotten and will suffer.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Concerning that which he previously was and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that which he is eternally - an unbegotten,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>impassible one from the Logos, who came into     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being in flesh - he did not come into their      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And this is the account which they received an   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>impulse to give concerning his flesh which was   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to appear.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They say that it is a production from all of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them, but that before all things it is from      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the spiritual Logos, who is the cause of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which have come into being, from whom     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Savior received his flesh.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He had conceived &lt;it&gt; at the revelation of the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>light, according to the word of the promise,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>at his revelation from the seminal state.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For the one who exists is not a seed of the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things which exist, since he was begotten at     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the end.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>But to the one by whom the Father ordained the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>manifestation of salvation, who is the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fulfillment of the promise, to him belonged      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>all these instruments for entry into life,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through which he descended.                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>His Father is one, and alone is truly a father   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to him, the invisible, unknowable, the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>incomprehensible in his nature, who alone is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>God in his will and his form, who has granted    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that he might be seen, known, and                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>comprehended.                                    |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>be conceived without sin, stain and              |

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>Mankind came to be in three essential types,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the spiritual, the psychic, and the material,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>conforming to the triple disposition of the      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Logos, from which were brought forth the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>material ones and the psychic ones and the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>spiritual ones.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Each of the three essential types is known by    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>its fruit.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And they were not known at first but only at     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the coming of the Savior, who shone upon the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>saints and revealed what each was.               |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The spiritual race, being like light from        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>light and like spirit from spirit, when its      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>head appeared, it ran toward him immediately.    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It immediately became a body of its head.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It suddenly received knowledge in the            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation.                                      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The psychic race is like light from a fire,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since it hesitated to accept knowledge of him    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who appeared to it.                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(It hesitated) even more to run toward him in    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>faith.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Rather, through a voice it was instructed, and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>this was sufficient, since it is not far from    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the hope according to the promise, since it      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received, so to speak as a pledge, the           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>assurance of the things which were to be.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The material race, however, is alien in every    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>way; since it is dark, it shuns the shining of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the light, because its appearance destroys it.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And since it has not received its unity, it is   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>something excessive and hateful toward the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Lord at his revelation.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The spiritual race will receive complete         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>salvation in every way.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The material will receive destruction in every   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>way, just as one who resists him.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The psychic race, since it is in the middle      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>when it is brought forth and also when it is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>created, is double according to its              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>determination for both good and evil.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It takes its appointed departure suddenly and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>its complete escape to those who are good.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those whom the Logos brought forth in            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>accordance with the first element of his         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought, when he remembered the exalted one      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and prayed for salvation, have salvation         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>suddenly.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They will be saved completely because of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>salvific thought.                                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As he was brought forth, so, too, were these     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought forth from him, whether angels or men.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>In accordance with the confession that there     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is one who is more exalted than themselves,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and in accordance with the prayer and the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>search for him, they also will attain the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>salvation of those who have been brought         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forth, since they are from the disposition       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is good.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They were appointed for service in proclaiming   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the coming of the Savior who was to be and his   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation which had come.                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Whether angels or men, when he was sent as a     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>service to them, they received, in fact, the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>essence of their being.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those, however, who are from the thought of      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>lust for power, who have come into being from    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the blow of those who fight against him, those   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom the thought brought forth, from these,      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since they are mixed, they will receive their    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>end suddenly.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those who will be brought forth from the lust    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for power which is given to them for a time      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and for certain periods, and who will give       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glory to the Lord of glory, and who will         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>relinquish their wrath, they will receive the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>reward for their humility, which is to remain    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>forever.                                         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those, however, who are proud because of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>desire of ambition, and who love temporary       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glory, and who forget that it was only for       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>certain periods and times which they have that   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they were entrusted with power, and for this     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>reason did not acknowledge that the Son of God   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is the Lord of all and Savior, and were not      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>brought out of wrath and the resemblance to      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the evil ones, they will receive judgment for    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their ignorance and their senselessness, which   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is suffering, along with those who went          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>astray, anyone of them who turned away; and      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>even more (for) wickedness in doing to the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Lord things which were not fitting, which the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>powers of the left did to him, even including    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>his death.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They persevered saying, &#34;We shall become         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>rulers of the universe, if the one who has       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>been proclaimed king of the universe is          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>slain,&#34; (they said this) when they labored to    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>do this, namely the men and angels who are not   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>from the good disposition of the right ones      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>but from the mixture.                            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And they first chose for themselves honor,       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>though it was only a temporary wish and          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>desire, while the path to eternal rest is by     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>way of humility for salvation of those who       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>will be saved, those of the right ones.          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>After they confess the Lord and the thought of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that which is pleasing to the church and the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>song of those who are humble along with her to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the full extent possible, in that which is       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>pleasing to do for her, in sharing in her        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sufferings and her pains in the manner of        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those who understand what is good for the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>church, they will have a share in her hope.      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is to be said on the subject of how men     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and angels who are from the order of the left    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>have a path to error: not only did they deny     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Lord and plot evil against him, but also     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>toward the Church did they direct their hatred   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and envy and jealousy; and this is the reason    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for the condemnation of those who have moved     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and have aroused themselves for the trials of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Church.                                      |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>
</div>

<td style="vertical-align:top;padding:0;margin:0;border:0;;width:100%">
<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>The election shares body and essence with the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Savior, since it is like a bridal chamber        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>because of its unity and its agreement with      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him.                                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For, before every place, the Christ came for     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>her sake.                                        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The calling, however, has the place of those     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who rejoice at the bridal chamber, and who are   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glad and happy at the union of the bridegroom    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the bride.                                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The place which the calling will have is the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>aeon of the images, where the Logos has not      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>yet joined with the Pleroma.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And since the man of the Church was happy and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>glad at this, as he was hoping for it, he        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>separated spirit, soul, and body in the          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>organization of the one who thinks that he is    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a unity, though within him is the man who is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Totality - and he is all of them.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And, though he has the escape from the [...]     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which the places will receive, he also has the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>members about which we spoke earlier.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>When the redemption was proclaimed, the          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>perfect man received knowledge immediately, so   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>as to return in haste to his unitary state, to   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the place from which he came, to return there    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>joyfully, to the place from which he came, to    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the place from which he flowed forth.            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>His members, however, needed a place of          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>instruction, which is in the places which are    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>adorned, so that they might receive from them    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>resemblance to the images and archetypes, like   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>a mirror, until all the members of the body of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Church are in a single place and receive     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the restoration at one time, when they have      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>been manifested as the whole body, namely the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>restoration into the Pleroma.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It has a preliminary concord with a mutual       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>agreement, which is the concord which belongs    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to the Father, until the Totalities receive a    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>countenance in accordance with him.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The restoration is at the end, after the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totality reveals what it is, the Son, who is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the redemption, that is, the path toward the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>incomprehensible Father, that is, the return     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to the pre-existent, and (after) the             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totalities reveal themselves in that one, in     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the proper way, who is the inconceivable one     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the ineffable one, and the invisible one     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the incomprehensible one, so that it         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>receives redemption.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It was not only release from the domination of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the left ones, nor was it only escape from the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>power of those of the right, to each of which    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>we thought that were slaves and sons, from       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>whom none escapes without quickly becoming       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>theirs again, but the redemption also is an      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ascent to the degrees which are in the Pleroma   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and to those who have named themselves and who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>conceive of themselves according to the power    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>of each of the aeons, and (it is) an entrance    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>into what is silent, where there is no need      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for voice nor for knowing, nor for forming a     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>concept, nor for illumination, but (where) all   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things are light, while they do not need to be   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>illumined.                                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Not only do humans need redemption, but also     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the angels, too, need redemption, along with     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the image and the rest of the Pleromas of the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>aeons and the wondrous powers of illumination.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>So that we might not be in doubt in regard to    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the others, even the Son himself, who has the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>position of redeemer of the Totality, needed     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>redemption as well, - he who had become man, -   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>since he gave himself for each thing which we    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>need, we in the flesh, who are his Church.       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Now, when he first received redemption from      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the word which had descended upon him, all the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>rest received redemption from him, namely        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those who had taken him to themselves.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>For those who received the one who had           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received (redemption) also received what was     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in him.                                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Among the men who are in the flesh redemption    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>began to be given, his first-born, and his       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>love, the Son who was incarnate, while the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>angels who are in heaven asked to associate,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>so that they might form an association with      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>him upon the earth.                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Therefore, he is called &#34;the Redemption of the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>angels of the Father,&#34; he who comforted those    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who were laboring under the Totality for his     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>knowledge, because he was given the grace        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>before anyone else.                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The Father had foreknowledge of him, since he    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was in his thought before anything came into     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>being, and since he had those to whom he has     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revealed him.                                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He set the deficiency on the one who remains     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for certain periods and times, as a glory for    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>his Pleroma, since the fact that he is unknown   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is a cause of his production from his            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>agreement [...] of him.                          |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Just as reception of knowledge of him is a       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>manifestation of his lack of envy and the        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation of the abundance of his sweetness,    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is the second glory, so, too, he has       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>been found to be a cause of ignorance,           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>although he is also a begetter of knowledge.     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>In a hidden and incomprehensible wisdom he       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>kept the knowledge to the end, until the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totalities became weary while searching for      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>God the Father, whom no one found through his    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>own wisdom or power.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He gives himself, so that they might receive     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>knowledge of the abundant thought about his      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>great glory, which he has given, and (about)     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the cause, which he has given, which is his      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>unceasing thanksgiving, he who, from the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>immobility of his counsel, reveals himself       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>eternally to those who have been worthy of the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father, who is unknown in his nature, so that    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>they might receive knowledge of him, through     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>his desire that they should come to experience   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the ignorance and its pains.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Those of whom he first thought that they         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>should attain knowledge and the good things      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which are in it, they were planning - which is   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the wisdom of the Father, - that they might      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>experience the evil things and might train       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>themselves in them, as a [...] for a time, so    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that they might receive the enjoyment of good    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>things for eternity.                             |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They hold change and persistent renunciation     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and the cause of those who fight against them    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>as an adornment and marvelous quality of those   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who are exalted, so that it is manifest that     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the ignorance of those who will be ignorant of   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the Father was something of their own.           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>He who gave them knowledge of him was one of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>his powers for enabling them to grasp that       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>knowledge in the fullest sense is called &#34;the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>knowledge of all that which is thought of&#34; and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;the treasure&#34; and &#34;the addition for the         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>increase of knowledge,&#34; &#34;the revelation of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those things which were known at first,&#34; and     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>&#34;the path toward harmony and toward the pre-     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>existent one,&#34; which is the increase of those    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>who have abandoned the greatness which was       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>theirs in the organization of the will, so       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>that the end might be like the beginning.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>As for the baptism which exists in the fullest   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sense, into which the Totalities will descend    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>and in which they will be, there is no other     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>baptism apart from this one alone, which is      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the redemption into God, Father, Son and Holy    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Spirit, when confession is made through faith    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>in those names, which are a single name of the   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>gospel, when they have come to believe what      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>has been said to them, namely that they exist.   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>From this they have their salvation, those who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>have believed that they exist.                   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is attaining in an invisible way to the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Father, Son, and Holy Spirit in an undoubting    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>faith.                                           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>And when they have borne witness to them, it     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is also with a firm hope that they attained      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them, so that the return to them might become    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the perfection of those who have believed in     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>them and (so that) the Father might be one       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>with them, the Father, the God, whom they have   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>confessed in faith and who gave (them) their     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>union with him in knowledge.                     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>The baptism which we previously mentioned is     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>called &#34;garment of those who do not strip        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>themselves of it,&#34; for those who will put it     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>on and those who have received redemption wear   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>it.                                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is also called &#34;the confirmation of the       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>truth which has no fall.&#34; In an unwavering and   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>immovable way it grasps those who have           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received the restoration while they grasp it.    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(Baptism) is called &#34;silence&#34; because of the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>quiet and the tranquility.                       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is also called &#34;bridal chamber&#34; because of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the agreement and the indivisible state of       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those who know they have known him.              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>It is also called &#34;the light which does not      |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>set and is without flame,&#34; since it does not     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>give light, but those who have worn it are       |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>made into light.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They are the ones whom he wore.                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>(Baptism) is also called &#34;the eternal life,&#34;     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is immortality; and it is called &#34;that     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>which is, entirely, simply, in the proper        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>sense, what is pleasing, inseparably and         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>irremovably and faultlessly and imperturbably,   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for the one who exists for those who have        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>received a beginning.&#34; For, what else is there   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>to name it apart from &#34;God,&#34; since it is the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Totalities, that is, even if it is given         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>numberless names, they are spoken simply as a    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>reference to it.                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Just as he transcends every word, and he         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>transcends every voice, and he transcends        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>every mind, and he transcends everything, and    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>he transcends every silence, so it is            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Dittography with those who are that which he     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is.                                              |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>This is that which they find it to be,           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>ineffably and inconceivably in (its) visage,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>for the coming into being in those who know,     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>through him whom they have comprehended, who     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>is the one to whom they gave glory.              |</span></span></code></pre></td></tr></table>
</div>

<pre tabindex="0" style="color:#f8f8f2;background-color:#272822;-moz-tab-size:4;-o-tab-size:4;tab-size:4;"><code class="language-text" data-lang="text"><span style="display:flex;"><span>Even if on the matter of the election there      |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>fitting to say, nonetheless, on the matter of    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>those of the calling - for those of the right    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>are so named - it is necessary for us to         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>return once again to them, and it is not         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>profitable for us to forget them.                |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>the exalted ones, or from the prayer and the     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>salvation from good work, since they have been   |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>good dispositions, (that) they have cause of     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>their begetting which is an opinion from the     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>one who exists.                                  |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Still further (I said) that before the Logos     |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>way, willingly, the exalted one added to this    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>thought, because they were in need of him, who   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>was the cause of their being.                    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>They did not exalt themselves when they were     |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>saved, as if there were nothing existing         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>before them, but they confess that they have a   |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>beginning to their existence, and they desire    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>this: to know him who exists before them.        |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>                                                 |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Most of all (I said) that they worshipped the    |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>revelation of the light in the form of           |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>lightning, and they bore witness that it         |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>appeared as &lt;their&gt; salvation.                   |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>would accomplish the good work, but also those   |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>dispositions will share in the repose            |
</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>according to the abundance of the grace.         |

</span></span><span style="display:flex;"><span>Also those who have been brought forth from      |
